# <a name="host-aspnet-core-on-windows-with-iis"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-103">Hospedar o ASP.NET Core no Windows com o IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-103">Host ASP.NET Core on Windows with IIS</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-5.0"

<span data-ttu-id="496af-104">O Serviços de Informações da Internet (IIS) é um servidor Web flexível, seguro e gerenciável para hospedar aplicativos Web, incluindo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-104">Internet Information Services (IIS) is a flexible, secure and manageable Web Server for hosting web apps, including ASP.NET Core.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="496af-107">Windows 7 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-107">Windows 7 or later</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="496af-108">Windows Server 2012 R2 ou posterior</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-108">Windows Server 2012 R2 or later</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-109">Aplicativos publicados para implantação de 32 bits (x86) ou 64 bits (x64) têm suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-109">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-110">Implantar um aplicativo de 32 bits com um SDK do .NET Core de 32 bits (x86), a menos que o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-110">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="496af-111">Exija o maior espaço de endereço de memória virtual disponível para um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-111">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="496af-112">Exija o maior tamanho de pilha do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-112">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="496af-113">Tenha dependências nativas de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-113">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

## <a name="supported-platforms"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-143">Plataformas com Suporte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-143">Supported platforms</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-144">Aplicativos publicados para implantação de 32 bits (x86) ou 64 bits (x64) têm suporte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-144">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) or 64-bit (x64) deployment are supported.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-145">Implantar um aplicativo de 32 bits com um SDK do .NET Core de 32 bits (x86), a menos que o aplicativo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-145">Deploy a 32-bit app with a 32-bit (x86) .NET Core SDK unless the app:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="496af-146">Exija o maior espaço de endereço de memória virtual disponível para um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-146">Requires the larger virtual memory address space available to a 64-bit app.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="496af-147">Exija o maior tamanho de pilha do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-147">Requires the larger IIS stack size.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="496af-148">Tenha dependências nativas de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-148">Has 64-bit native dependencies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-149">Os aplicativos publicados para 32 bits (x86) devem ter 32 bits habilitado para seus pools de aplicativos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-149">Apps published for 32-bit (x86) must have 32-bit enabled for their IIS Application Pools.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-150">Para obter mais informações, consulte a seção [criar o site do IIS](#create-the-iis-site) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-150">For more information, see the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-151">Use um SDK do .NET Core de 64 bits (x64) para publicar um aplicativo de 64 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-151">Use a 64-bit (x64) .NET Core SDK to publish a 64-bit app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-152">Um runtime de 64 bits deve estar presente no sistema host.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-152">A 64-bit runtime must be present on the host system.</span></span>

## <a name="hosting-models"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-153">Modelos de hospedagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-153">Hosting models</span></span>

### <a name="in-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-154">Modelo de hospedagem em processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-154">In-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-155">Usando uma hospedagem em processo, um aplicativo ASP.NET Core é executado no mesmo processo que seu processo de trabalho do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-155">Using in-process hosting, an ASP.NET Core app runs in the same process as its IIS worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-156">A hospedagem em processo oferece desempenho melhor em hospedagem fora do processo porque as solicitações não são transmitidas por proxy pelo adaptador de loopback, um adaptador de rede que retorna o tráfego de rede de saída para o mesmo computador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-156">In-process hosting provides improved performance over out-of-process hosting because requests aren't proxied over the loopback adapter, a network interface that returns outgoing network traffic back to the same machine.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-157">O IIS manipula o gerenciamento de processos com o [WAS (Serviço de Ativação de Processos do Windows)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-157">IIS handles process management with the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-158">O [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-158">The [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module):</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="496af-159">Executa a inicialização do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-159">Performs app initialization.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="496af-160">Carrega o [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-160">Loads the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr).</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="496af-161">Chama `Program.Main`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-161">Calls `Program.Main`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="496af-162">Manipula o tempo de vida da solicitação nativa do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-162">Handles the lifetime of the IIS native request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-163">O diagrama a seguir ilustra a relação entre o IIS, o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e um aplicativo hospedado em processo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-163">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted in-process:</span></span>

![Módulo do ASP.NET Core no cenário de hospedagem em processo](index/_static/ancm-inprocess.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-165">A solicitação chega da Web para o driver do HTTP.sys no modo kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-165">A request arrives from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-166">O driver roteia as solicitações nativas ao IIS na porta configurada do site, normalmente, a 80 (HTTP) ou a 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-166">The driver routes the native request to IIS on the website's configured port, usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-167">O módulo ASP.NET Core recebe a solicitação nativa e a passa para o servidor HTTP IIS ( `IISHttpServer` ).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-167">The ASP.NET Core Module receives the native request and passes it to IIS HTTP Server (`IISHttpServer`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-168">O servidor HTTP do IIS é uma implementação de servidor em processo do IIS que converte a solicitação de nativa para gerenciada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-168">IIS HTTP Server is an in-process server implementation for IIS that converts the request from native to managed.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-169">Depois que o servidor HTTP IIS processar a solicitação:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-169">After the IIS HTTP Server processes the request:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-170">A solicitação é enviada para o pipeline de middleware ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-170">The request is sent to the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-171">O pipeline do middleware manipula a solicitação e a passa como uma instância de `HttpContext` para a lógica do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-171">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-172">A resposta do aplicativo é retornada ao IIS por meio do Servidor HTTP do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-172">The app's response is passed back to IIS through IIS HTTP Server.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-173">O IIS enviará a resposta ao cliente que iniciou a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-173">IIS sends the response to the client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-174">A hospedagem em processo é opcional para aplicativos existentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-174">In-process hosting is opt-in for existing apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-175">Os modelos da Web ASP.NET Core usam o modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-175">The ASP.NET Core web templates use the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-176">`CreateDefaultBuilder` Adiciona uma <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> instância chamando o <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS%2A> método para inicializar o [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) e hospedar o aplicativo dentro do processo de trabalho do IIS ( `w3wp.exe` ou `iisexpress.exe` ).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-176">`CreateDefaultBuilder` adds an <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.Server.IServer> instance by calling the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIIS%2A> method to boot the [CoreCLR](/dotnet/standard/glossary#coreclr) and host the app inside of the IIS worker process (`w3wp.exe` or `iisexpress.exe`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-177">Os testes de desempenho indicam que hospedar um aplicativo em processo do .NET Core oferece uma de taxa de transferência de solicitação significativamente mais elevada em comparação a hospedar o aplicativo fora do processo e enviar por proxy as solicitações para o [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-177">Performance tests indicate that hosting a .NET Core app in-process delivers significantly higher request throughput compared to hosting the app out-of-process and proxying requests to [Kestrel](xref:fundamentals/servers/kestrel).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-178">Aplicativos publicados como um único arquivo executável não podem ser carregados pelo modelo de hospedagem em processo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-178">Apps published as a single file executable can't be loaded by the in-process hosting model.</span></span>

### <a name="out-of-process-hosting-model"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-179">Modelo de hospedagem de fora do processo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-179">Out-of-process hosting model</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-180">Como ASP.NET Core aplicativos são executados em um processo separado do processo de trabalho do IIS, o módulo ASP.NET Core lida com o gerenciamento de processos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-180">Because ASP.NET Core apps run in a process separate from the IIS worker process, the ASP.NET Core Module handles process management.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-181">O módulo inicia o processo para o aplicativo ASP.NET Core quando a primeira solicitação chega e reinicia o aplicativo se ele é desligado ou falha.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-181">The module starts the process for the ASP.NET Core app when the first request arrives and restarts the app if it shuts down or crashes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-182">Isso é basicamente o mesmo comportamento que o dos aplicativos que são executados dentro do processo e são gerenciados pelo [WAS (Serviço de Ativação de Processos do Windows)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-182">This is essentially the same behavior as seen with apps that run in-process that are managed by the [Windows Process Activation Service (WAS)](/iis/manage/provisioning-and-managing-iis/features-of-the-windows-process-activation-service-was).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-183">O diagrama a seguir ilustra a relação entre o IIS, o Módulo do ASP.NET Core e um aplicativo hospedado de fora d processo:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-183">The following diagram illustrates the relationship between IIS, the ASP.NET Core Module, and an app hosted out-of-process:</span></span>

![Módulo do ASP.NET Core no cenário de hospedagem fora do processo](index/_static/ancm-outofprocess.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-185">As solicitações chegam da Web para o driver do HTTP.sys no modo kernel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-185">Requests arrive from the web to the kernel-mode HTTP.sys driver.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-186">O driver roteia as solicitações para o IIS na porta configurada do site.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-186">The driver routes the requests to IIS on the website's configured port.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-187">A porta configurada geralmente é 80 (HTTP) ou 443 (HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-187">The configured port is usually 80 (HTTP) or 443 (HTTPS).</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-188">O módulo encaminha as solicitações para Kestrel em uma porta aleatória para o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-188">The module forwards the requests to Kestrel on a random port for the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-189">A porta aleatória não é 80 ou 443.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-189">The random port isn't 80 or 443.</span></span>

<!-- make this a bullet list -->
<span data-ttu-id="496af-190">O módulo ASP.NET Core especifica a porta por meio de uma variável de ambiente na inicialização.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-190">The ASP.NET Core Module specifies the port via an environment variable at startup.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-191">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration%2A> extensão configura o servidor a ser escutado `http://localhost:{PORT}` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-191">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.WebHostBuilderIISExtensions.UseIISIntegration%2A> extension configures the server to listen on `http://localhost:{PORT}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-192">Outras verificações são executadas e as solicitações que não se originam do módulo são rejeitadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-192">Additional checks are performed, and requests that don't originate from the module are rejected.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-193">O módulo não dá suporte ao encaminhamento de HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-193">The module doesn't support HTTPS forwarding.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-194">As solicitações são encaminhadas por HTTP, mesmo se recebidas pelo IIS sobre HTTPS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-194">Requests are forwarded over HTTP even if received by IIS over HTTPS.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-195">Depois que o Kestrel pega a solicitação do módulo, a solicitação é encaminhada para o pipeline de middleware ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-195">After Kestrel picks up the request from the module, the request is forwarded into the ASP.NET Core middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-196">O pipeline do middleware manipula a solicitação e a passa como uma instância de `HttpContext` para a lógica do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-196">The middleware pipeline handles the request and passes it on as an `HttpContext` instance to the app's logic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-197">O middleware adicionado pela integração do IIS atualiza o esquema, o IP remoto e pathbase para encaminhar a solicitação para o Kestrel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-197">Middleware added by IIS Integration updates the scheme, remote IP, and pathbase to account for forwarding the request to Kestrel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-198">A resposta do aplicativo é passada de volta para o IIS, que o encaminha de volta para o cliente HTTP que iniciou a solicitação.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-198">The app's response is passed back to IIS, which forwards it back to the HTTP client that initiated the request.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-199">Para orientação sobre a configuração do Módulo do ASP.NET Core, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-199">For ASP.NET Core Module configuration guidance, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-200">Para saber mais sobre hospedagem, confira [Host no ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-200">For more information on hosting, see [Host in ASP.NET Core](xref:fundamentals/index#host).</span></span>

## <a name="application-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-201">Configuração de aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-201">Application configuration</span></span>

### <a name="enable-the-iisintegration-components"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-202">Habilitar os componentes de IISIntegration</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-202">Enable the IISIntegration components</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-203">Ao criar um host no `CreateHostBuilder` ( `Program.cs` ), chame <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder%2A> para habilitar a integração do IIS:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-203">When building a host in `CreateHostBuilder` (`Program.cs`), call <xref:Microsoft.Extensions.Hosting.Host.CreateDefaultBuilder%2A> to enable IIS integration:</span></span>

```csharp
public static IHostBuilder CreateHostBuilder(string[] args) =>
    Host.CreateDefaultBuilder(args)
        ...
```

<span data-ttu-id="496af-204">Para obter mais informações sobre o `CreateDefaultBuilder`, consulte <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-204">For more information on `CreateDefaultBuilder`, see <xref:fundamentals/host/generic-host#default-builder-settings>.</span></span>

### <a name="iis-options"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-205">Opções do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-205">IIS options</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-206">**Modelo de hospedagem em processo**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-206">**In-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-207">Para configurar as opções do Servidor IIS, inclua uma configuração de serviço para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices%2A>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-207">To configure IIS Server options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISServerOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices%2A>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-208">O exemplo a seguir desabilita AutomaticAuthentication:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-208">The following example disables AutomaticAuthentication:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISServerOptions>(options => 
{
    options.AutomaticAuthentication = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="496af-209">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-209">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="496af-210">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-210">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="496af-211">Configuração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-211">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="496af-212">Se `true`, o Servidor do IIS define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-212">If `true`, IIS Server sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-213">Se `false`, o servidor fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-213">If `false`, the server only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-214">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-214">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-215">Para obter mais informações, veja [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-215">For more information, see [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="496af-216">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-216">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `AllowSynchronousIO`           | `false` | <span data-ttu-id="496af-217">Se a e/s síncrona é permitida para o `HttpContext.Request` e o `HttpContext.Response` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-217">Whether synchronous I/O is allowed for the `HttpContext.Request` and the `HttpContext.Response`.</span></span> |
| `MaxRequestBodySize`           | `30000000`  | <span data-ttu-id="496af-218">Obtém ou define o tamanho máximo do corpo da solicitação para o `HttpRequest`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-218">Gets or sets the max request body size for the `HttpRequest`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-219">Observe que o próprio IIS tem o limite `maxAllowedContentLength` que será processado antes de `MaxRequestBodySize` definido no `IISServerOptions`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-219">Note that IIS itself has the limit `maxAllowedContentLength` which will be processed before the `MaxRequestBodySize` set in the `IISServerOptions`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-220">Alterar `MaxRequestBodySize` não afetará `maxAllowedContentLength`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-220">Changing the `MaxRequestBodySize` won't affect the `maxAllowedContentLength`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-221">Para aumentar `maxAllowedContentLength` , adicione uma entrada no `web.config` para definir `maxAllowedContentLength` como um valor mais alto.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-221">To increase `maxAllowedContentLength`, add an entry in the `web.config` to set `maxAllowedContentLength` to a higher value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-222">Para obter mais detalhes, confira [Configuração](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-222">For more details, see [Configuration](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/requestFiltering/requestLimits/#configuration).</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="496af-223">**Modelo de hospedagem de fora do processo**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-223">**Out-of-process hosting model**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-224">Para configurar opções do IIS, inclua uma configuração de serviço para <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> em <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices%2A>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-224">To configure IIS options, include a service configuration for <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IISOptions> in <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Hosting.IStartup.ConfigureServices%2A>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-225">O exemplo a seguir impede que o aplicativo preencha `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-225">The following example prevents the app from populating `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.Configure<IISOptions>(options => 
{
    options.ForwardClientCertificate = false;
});
```

| <span data-ttu-id="496af-226">Opção</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-226">Option</span></span>                         | <span data-ttu-id="496af-227">Padrão</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-227">Default</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="496af-228">Configuração</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-228">Setting</span></span> |
| ------------------------------ | :-----: | ------- |
| `AutomaticAuthentication`      | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="496af-229">Se `true`, o [middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) define o `HttpContext.User` autenticado pela [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-229">If `true`, [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) sets the `HttpContext.User` authenticated by [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-230">Se `false`, o middleware fornecerá apenas uma identidade para `HttpContext.User` e responderá a desafios quando explicitamente solicitado pelo `AuthenticationScheme`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-230">If `false`, the middleware only provides an identity for `HttpContext.User` and responds to challenges when explicitly requested by the `AuthenticationScheme`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-231">A autenticação do Windows deve estar habilitada no IIS para que o `AutomaticAuthentication` funcione.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-231">Windows Authentication must be enabled in IIS for `AutomaticAuthentication` to function.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-232">Saiba mais no tópico [Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-232">For more information, see the [Windows Authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth) topic.</span></span> |
| `AuthenticationDisplayName`    | `null`  | <span data-ttu-id="496af-233">Configura o nome de exibição mostrado aos usuários em páginas de logon.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-233">Sets the display name shown to users on login pages.</span></span> |
| `ForwardClientCertificate`     | `true`  | <span data-ttu-id="496af-234">Se `true` e o cabeçalho da solicitação `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` estiverem presentes, o `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` será populado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-234">If `true` and the `MS-ASPNETCORE-CLIENTCERT` request header is present, the `HttpContext.Connection.ClientCertificate` is populated.</span></span> |

### <a name="proxy-server-and-load-balancer-scenarios"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-235">Servidor proxy e cenários de balanceador de carga</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-235">Proxy server and load balancer scenarios</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-236">O [middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) e o módulo ASP.NET Core são configurados para encaminhar o:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-236">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) and the ASP.NET Core Module are configured to forward the:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="496af-237">Esquema (HTTP/HTTPS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-237">Scheme (HTTP/HTTPS).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="496af-238">Endereço IP remoto em que a solicitação foi originada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-238">Remote IP address where the request originated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-239">O [middleware de integração do IIS](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configura o middleware de cabeçalhos encaminhados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-239">The [IIS Integration Middleware](#enable-the-iisintegration-components) configures Forwarded Headers Middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-240">Configuração adicional pode ser necessária para aplicativos hospedados atrás de servidores proxy adicionais e balanceadores de carga.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-240">Additional configuration might be required for apps hosted behind additional proxy servers and load balancers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-241">Para obter mais informações, veja [Configurar o ASP.NET Core para trabalhar com servidores proxy e balanceadores de carga](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-241">For more information, see [Configure ASP.NET Core to work with proxy servers and load balancers](xref:host-and-deploy/proxy-load-balancer).</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-242">Arquivo `web.config`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-242">`web.config` file</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-243">O `web.config` arquivo configura o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-243">The `web.config` file configures the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-244">Criar, transformar e publicar o `web.config` arquivo é tratado por um destino do MSBuild ( `_TransformWebConfig` ) quando o projeto é publicado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-244">Creating, transforming, and publishing the `web.config` file is handled by an MSBuild target (`_TransformWebConfig`) when the project is published.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-245">Este destino está presente nos destinos do SDK da Web (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-245">This target is present in the Web SDK targets (`Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-246">O SDK é definido na parte superior do arquivo de projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-246">The SDK is set at the top of the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<Project Sdk="Microsoft.NET.Sdk.Web">
```

<span data-ttu-id="496af-247">Se um `web.config` arquivo não estiver presente no projeto, o arquivo será criado com o correto `processPath` e `arguments` para configurar o módulo ASP.NET Core e movido para a [saída publicada](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-247">If a `web.config` file isn't present in the project, the file is created with the correct `processPath` and `arguments` to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to [published output](xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-248">Se um `web.config` arquivo estiver presente no projeto, o arquivo será transformado com o correto `processPath` e `arguments` para configurar o módulo ASP.NET Core e movido para a saída publicada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-248">If a `web.config` file is present in the project, the file is transformed with the correct `processPath` and `arguments` to configure the ASP.NET Core Module and moved to published output.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-249">A transformação não altera as definições de configuração do IIS no arquivo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-249">The transformation doesn't modify IIS configuration settings in the file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-250">O `web.config` arquivo pode fornecer definições de configuração adicionais do IIS que controlam os módulos do IIS ativos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-250">The `web.config` file may provide additional IIS configuration settings that control active IIS modules.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-251">Para saber mais sobre os módulos do IIS que podem processar solicitações com aplicativos do ASP.NET Core, veja o tópico [Módulos do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-251">For information on IIS modules that are capable of processing requests with ASP.NET Core apps, see the [IIS modules](xref:host-and-deploy/iis/modules) topic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-252">Para impedir que o SDK da Web transforme o `web.config` arquivo, use a `<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>` propriedade no arquivo de projeto:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-252">To prevent the Web SDK from transforming the `web.config` file, use the `<IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>` property in the project file:</span></span>

```xml
<PropertyGroup>
  <IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>true</IsTransformWebConfigDisabled>
</PropertyGroup>
```

<span data-ttu-id="496af-253">Ao desabilitar o SDK da Web da transformação do arquivo, o e o `processPath` `arguments` devem ser definidos manualmente pelo desenvolvedor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-253">When disabling the Web SDK from transforming the file, the `processPath` and `arguments` should be manually set by the developer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-254">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-254">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module>.</span></span>

### <a name="webconfig-file-location"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-255">`web.config` local do arquivo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-255">`web.config` file location</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-256">Para configurar o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) corretamente, o `web.config` arquivo deve estar presente no caminho [raiz do conteúdo](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) (normalmente o caminho base do aplicativo) do aplicativo implantado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-256">In order to set up the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module) correctly, the `web.config` file must be present at the [content root](xref:fundamentals/index#content-root) path (typically the app base path) of the deployed app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-257">Esse é o mesmo local que o caminho físico do site fornecido ao IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-257">This is the same location as the website physical path provided to IIS.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-258">O `web.config` arquivo é necessário na raiz do aplicativo para habilitar a publicação de vários aplicativos usando implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-258">The `web.config` file is required at the root of the app to enable the publishing of multiple apps using Web Deploy.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-259">Existem arquivos confidenciais no caminho físico do aplicativo, como `{ASSEMBLY}.runtimeconfig.json` `{ASSEMBLY}.xml` (comentários de documentação XML) e `{ASSEMBLY}.deps.json` , em que o espaço reservado `{ASSEMBLY}` é o nome do assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-259">Sensitive files exist on the app's physical path, such as `{ASSEMBLY}.runtimeconfig.json`, `{ASSEMBLY}.xml` (XML Documentation comments), and `{ASSEMBLY}.deps.json`, where the placeholder `{ASSEMBLY}` is the assembly name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-260">Quando o `web.config` arquivo estiver presente e o site for iniciado normalmente, o IIS não atenderá a esses arquivos confidenciais se eles forem solicitados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-260">When the `web.config` file is present and the site starts normally, IIS doesn't serve these sensitive files if they're requested.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-261">Se o `web.config` arquivo estiver ausente, incorretamente nomeado ou não for possível configurar o site para inicialização normal, o IIS poderá fornecer arquivos confidenciais publicamente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-261">If the `web.config` file is missing, incorrectly named, or unable to configure the site for normal startup, IIS may serve sensitive files publicly.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-262">**O `web.config` arquivo deve estar presente na implantação em todos os momentos, corretamente nomeado e ser capaz de configurar o site para inicialização normal. Nunca remova o `web.config` arquivo de uma implantação de produção.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-262">**The `web.config` file must be present in the deployment at all times, correctly named, and able to configure the site for normal start up. Never remove the `web.config` file from a production deployment.**</span></span>

### <a name="transform-webconfig"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-263">Transformação do Web.config</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-263">Transform web.config</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-264">Se você precisar transformar `web.config` em publicar, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-264">If you need to transform `web.config` on publish, see <xref:host-and-deploy/iis/transform-webconfig>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-265">Talvez seja necessário transformar `web.config` em publicar para definir variáveis de ambiente com base na configuração, no perfil ou no ambiente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-265">You might need to transform `web.config` on publish to set environment variables based on the configuration, profile, or environment.</span></span>

## <a name="iis-configuration"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-266">Configuração do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-266">IIS configuration</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-267">**Sistemas operacionais do Windows Server**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-267">**Windows Server operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-268">Habilite a função **Servidor Web (IIS)** e estabeleça serviços de função.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-268">Enable the **Web Server (IIS)** server role and establish role services.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-269">Use o assistente **Adicionar Funções e Recursos** por meio do menu **Gerenciar** ou do link no **Gerenciador do Servidor**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-269">Use the **Add Roles and Features** wizard from the **Manage** menu or the link in **Server Manager**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-270">Na etapa **Funções de Servidor**, marque a caixa de **Servidor Web (IIS)**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-270">On the **Server Roles** step, check the box for **Web Server (IIS)**.</span></span>

   ![A função de Servidor Web IIS é selecionada na etapa Selecionar funções de servidor.](index/_static/server-roles-ws2016.png)

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-272">Após a etapa **Recursos**, a etapa **Serviços de função** é carregada para o servidor Web (IIS).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-272">After the **Features** step, the **Role services** step loads for Web Server (IIS).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-273">Selecione os serviços de função do IIS desejados ou aceite os serviços de função padrão fornecidos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-273">Select the IIS role services desired or accept the default role services provided.</span></span>

   ![Os serviços de função padrão são selecionados na etapa Selecionar serviços de função.](index/_static/role-services-ws2016.png)

   <span data-ttu-id="496af-275">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-275">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="496af-276">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós: segurança do **servidor Web**  >  .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-276">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-277">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-277">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-278">Para obter mais informações, consulte [autenticação `<windowsAuthentication>` do Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar a autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-278">For more information, see [Windows Authentication `<windowsAuthentication>`](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="496af-279">**WebSockets (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-279">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="496af-280">O WebSockets é compatível com o ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-280">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-281">Para habilitar WebSockets, expanda os seguintes nós: desenvolvimento de aplicativo de **servidor Web**  >  .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-281">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **Web Server** > **Application Development**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-282">Selecione o recurso **Protocolo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-282">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-283">Para obter mais informações, consulte [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-283">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-284">Continue para a etapa **Confirmação** para instalar os serviços e a função de servidor Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-284">Proceed through the **Confirmation** step to install the web server role and services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-285">Uma reinicialização de servidor/IIS não é necessária após a instalação da função do **servidor Web (IIS)** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-285">A server/IIS restart isn't required after installing the **Web Server (IIS)** role.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-286">**Sistemas operacionais de área de trabalho do Windows**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-286">**Windows desktop operating systems**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-287">Habilite o **Console de Gerenciamento do IIS** e os **Serviços na World Wide Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-287">Enable the **IIS Management Console** and **World Wide Web Services**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-289">Abra o nó **Serviços de Informações da Internet**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-289">Open the **Internet Information Services** node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-290">Abra o nó **Ferramentas de Gerenciamento da Web**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-290">Open the **Web Management Tools** node.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-293">Aceite os recursos padrão dos **Serviços na World Wide Web** ou personalize os recursos do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-293">Accept the default features for **World Wide Web Services** or customize the IIS features.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="496af-294">**Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-294">**Windows Authentication (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="496af-295">Para habilitar a autenticação do Windows, expanda os seguintes nós: segurança **dos serviços de World Wide Web**  >  .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-295">To enable Windows Authentication, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Security**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-296">Selecione o recurso **Autenticação do Windows**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-296">Select the **Windows Authentication** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-297">Para obter mais informações, consulte [autenticação \<windowsAuthentication> do Windows](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) e [Configurar a autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-297">For more information, see [Windows Authentication \<windowsAuthentication>](/iis/configuration/system.webServer/security/authentication/windowsAuthentication/) and [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="496af-298">**WebSockets (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-298">**WebSockets (Optional)**</span></span>  
   <span data-ttu-id="496af-299">O WebSockets é compatível com o ASP.NET Core 1.1 ou posterior.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-299">WebSockets is supported with ASP.NET Core 1.1 or later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-300">Para habilitar WebSockets, expanda os seguintes nós: recursos de desenvolvimento de aplicativos **World Wide Web Services**  >  .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-300">To enable WebSockets, expand the following nodes: **World Wide Web Services** > **Application Development Features**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-301">Selecione o recurso **Protocolo WebSocket**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-301">Select the **WebSocket Protocol** feature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-302">Para obter mais informações, consulte [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-302">For more information, see [WebSockets](xref:fundamentals/websockets).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-303">Se a instalação do IIS exigir uma reinicialização, reinicie o sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-303">If the IIS installation requires a restart, restart the system.</span></span>

## <a name="install-the-net-core-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-305">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-305">Install the .NET Core Hosting Bundle</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-306">Instale o *pacote de hospedagem do .NET Core* no sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-306">Install the *.NET Core Hosting Bundle* on the hosting system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-307">O pacote instala o tempo de execução do .NET Core, a biblioteca do .NET Core e o [módulo ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-307">The bundle installs the .NET Core Runtime, .NET Core Library, and the [ASP.NET Core Module](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-308">O módulo permite que aplicativos do ASP.NET Core sejam executados por trás do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-308">The module allows ASP.NET Core apps to run behind IIS.</span></span>

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="496af-309">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado antes do IIS, a instalação do pacote deverá ser reparada.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-309">If the Hosting Bundle is installed before IIS, the bundle installation must be repaired.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-310">Execute o instalador do pacote de hospedagem novamente depois de instalar o IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-310">Run the Hosting Bundle installer again after installing IIS.</span></span>
>
> <span data-ttu-id="496af-311">Se o pacote de hospedagem for instalado após a instalação da versão de 64 bits (x64) do .NET Core, os SDKs poderão parecer estar ausentes ([Nenhum SDK do .NET Core foi detectado](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-311">If the Hosting Bundle is installed after installing the 64-bit (x64) version of .NET Core, SDKs might appear to be missing ([No .NET Core SDKs were detected](xref:test/troubleshoot#no-net-core-sdks-were-detected)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-312">Para resolver o problema, consulte <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-312">To resolve the problem, see <xref:test/troubleshoot#missing-sdk-after-installing-the-net-core-hosting-bundle>.</span></span>

### <a name="install-the-hosting-bundle"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-324">Instalar o pacote de hospedagem</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-324">Install the Hosting Bundle</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-325">Execute o instalador no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-325">Run the installer on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-326">Os parâmetros a seguir estão disponíveis ao executar o instalador por meio de um shell de comando do administrador:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-326">The following parameters are available when running the installer from an administrator command shell:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="496af-327">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Ignorar a instalação do módulo ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-327">`OPT_NO_ANCM=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Core Module.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="496af-328">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Ignorar a instalação do tempo de execução do .NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-328">`OPT_NO_RUNTIME=1`: Skip installing the .NET Core runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-329">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-329">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="496af-330">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Ignorar a instalação da estrutura compartilhada ASP.NET (ASP.NET Runtime).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-330">`OPT_NO_SHAREDFX=1`: Skip installing the ASP.NET Shared Framework (ASP.NET runtime).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-331">Usado quando o servidor hospeda apenas [implantações independentes (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-331">Used when the server only hosts [self-contained deployments (SCD)](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd).</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="496af-332">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Ignorar a instalação de tempos de execução x86.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-332">`OPT_NO_X86=1`: Skip installing x86 runtimes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-333">Use esse parâmetro quando você souber que não hospedará aplicativos de 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-333">Use this parameter when you know that you won't be hosting 32-bit apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-334">Se houver uma possibilidade de hospedar aplicativos de 32 bits e 64 bits no futuro, não use esse parâmetro e instale ambos os runtimes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-334">If there's any chance that you will host both 32-bit and 64-bit apps in the future, don't use this parameter and install both runtimes.</span></span>
   * <span data-ttu-id="496af-335">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Desabilite a verificação para usar uma configuração compartilhada do IIS quando a configuração compartilhada ( `applicationHost.config` ) estiver no mesmo computador que a instalação do IIS.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-335">`OPT_NO_SHARED_CONFIG_CHECK=1`: Disable the check for using an IIS Shared Configuration when the shared configuration (`applicationHost.config`) is on the same machine as the IIS installation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-336">*Disponível somente para instaladores do ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou Hosting Bundler posterior.*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-336">*Only available for ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later Hosting Bundler installers.*</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-337">Para obter mais informações, consulte <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-337">For more information, see <xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration>.</span></span>
1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-338">Reinicie o sistema ou execute os seguintes comandos em um shell de comando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-338">Restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

   ```console
   net stop was /y
   net start w3svc
   ```
   <span data-ttu-id="496af-339">A reinicialização do IIS identifica uma alteração no CAMINHO do sistema, que é uma variável de ambiente, realizada pelo instalador.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-339">Restarting IIS picks up a change to the system PATH, which is an environment variable, made by the installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-340">ASP.NET Core não adota o comportamento de roll-forward para versões de patch de pacotes de estrutura compartilhados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-340">ASP.NET Core doesn't adopt roll-forward behavior for patch releases of shared framework packages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-341">Depois de atualizar a estrutura compartilhada instalando um novo pacote de hospedagem, reinicie o sistema ou execute os seguintes comandos em um shell de comando:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-341">After upgrading the shared framework by installing a new hosting bundle, restart the system or execute the following commands in a command shell:</span></span>

```console
net stop was /y
net start w3svc
```

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="496af-342">Para obter informações sobre a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS, consulte [Módulo do ASP.NET Core com a Configuração Compartilhada do IIS](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-342">For information on IIS Shared Configuration, see [ASP.NET Core Module with IIS Shared Configuration](xref:host-and-deploy/aspnet-core-module#aspnet-core-module-with-an-iis-shared-configuration).</span></span>

## <a name="install-web-deploy-when-publishing-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-343">Instalar a Implantação da Web durante a publicação com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-343">Install Web Deploy when publishing with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-344">Ao implantar aplicativos para servidores com [Implantação da Web](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), instale a versão mais recente da Implantação da Web no servidor.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-344">When deploying apps to servers with [Web Deploy](/iis/install/installing-publishing-technologies/installing-and-configuring-web-deploy-on-iis-80-or-later), install the latest version of Web Deploy on the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-345">Para instalar a Implantação da Web, use o [WebPI (Web Platform Installer)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) ou obtenha um instalador diretamente no [Centro de Download da Microsoft](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-345">To install Web Deploy, use the [Web Platform Installer (WebPI)](https://www.microsoft.com/web/downloads/platform.aspx) or obtain an installer directly from the [Microsoft Download Center](https://www.microsoft.com/download/details.aspx?id=43717).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-346">O método preferencial é usar o WebPI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-346">The preferred method is to use WebPI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-347">O WebPI oferece uma instalação autônoma e uma configuração para provedores de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-347">WebPI offers a standalone setup and a configuration for hosting providers.</span></span>

## <a name="create-the-iis-site"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-348">Criar o site do IIS</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-348">Create the IIS site</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-349">No sistema de hospedagem, crie uma pasta para conter arquivos e pastas publicados do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-349">On the hosting system, create a folder to contain the app's published folders and files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-350">Em uma etapa a seguir, o caminho da pasta é fornecido ao IIS como o caminho físico para o aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-350">In a following step, the folder's path is provided to IIS as the physical path to the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-351">Para obter mais informações sobre o layout de arquivo e a pasta de implantação de um aplicativo, confira <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-351">For more information on an app's deployment folder and file layout, see <xref:host-and-deploy/directory-structure>.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-352">No Gerenciador do IIS, abra o nó do servidor no painel **conexões** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-352">In IIS Manager, open the server's node in the **Connections** panel.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-353">Clique com botão direito do mouse na pasta **Sites**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-353">Right-click the **Sites** folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-354">Selecione **Adicionar Site** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-354">Select **Add Website** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-355">Forneça um **Nome do site** e defina o **Caminho físico** como a pasta de implantação do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-355">Provide a **Site name** and set the **Physical path** to the app's deployment folder.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-356">Forneça a configuração de **Associação** e crie o site selecionando **OK**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-356">Provide the **Binding** configuration and create the website by selecting **OK**:</span></span>

   ![Forneça o Nome do site, o caminho físico e o Nome do host na etapa Adicionar Site.](index/_static/add-website-ws2016.png)

   > [!WARNING]
   > <span data-ttu-id="496af-358">Associações de curinga de nível superior (`http://*:80/` e `http://+:80`) **não** devem ser usadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-358">Top-level wildcard bindings (`http://*:80/` and `http://+:80`) should **not** be used.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-359">Associações de curinga de nível superior podem abrir o aplicativo para vulnerabilidades de segurança.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-359">Top-level wildcard bindings can open up your app to security vulnerabilities.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-360">Isso se aplica a curingas fortes e fracos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-360">This applies to both strong and weak wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-361">Use nomes de host explícitos em vez de curingas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-361">Use explicit host names rather than wildcards.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-362">Associações de curinga de subdomínio (por exemplo, `*.mysub.com`) não têm esse risco de segurança se você controlar o domínio pai completo (em vez de `*.com`, o qual é vulnerável).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-362">Subdomain wildcard binding (for example, `*.mysub.com`) doesn't have this security risk if you control the entire parent domain (as opposed to `*.com`, which is vulnerable).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-363">Veja [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) para obter mais informações.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-363">See [rfc7230 section-5.4](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc7230#section-5.4) for more information.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-364">No nó do servidor, selecione **Pools de Aplicativos**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-364">Under the server's node, select **Application Pools**.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-365">Clique com o botão direito do mouse no pool de aplicativos do site e selecione **Configurações Básicas** no menu contextual.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-365">Right-click the site's app pool and select **Basic Settings** from the contextual menu.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-366">Na janela **Editar Pool de Aplicativos**, defina a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado**:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-366">In the **Edit Application Pool** window, set the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code**:</span></span>

   ![Defina Sem Código Gerenciado para a versão do CLR do .NET.](index/_static/edit-apppool-ws2016.png)

    <span data-ttu-id="496af-368">O ASP.NET Core é executado em um processo separado e gerencia o runtime.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-368">ASP.NET Core runs in a separate process and manages the runtime.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-369">ASP.NET Core não depende do carregamento do CLR da área de trabalho (.NET CLR).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-369">ASP.NET Core doesn't rely on loading the desktop CLR (.NET CLR).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-370">O principal CoreCLR (Common Language Runtime) para .NET Core é inicializado para hospedar o aplicativo no processo de trabalho.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-370">The Core Common Language Runtime (CoreCLR) for .NET Core is booted to host the app in the worker process.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-371">Definir a **versão do CLR do .NET** como **Sem Código Gerenciado** é opcional, porém recomendado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-371">Setting the **.NET CLR version** to **No Managed Code** is optional but recommended.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-372">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 ou posterior*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-372">*ASP.NET Core 2.2 or later*:</span></span>

   * <span data-ttu-id="496af-373">Para uma [implantação autônoma](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) de 32 bits (x86) publicada com um SDK de 32 bits que usa o modelo de [hospedagem em processo](#in-process-hosting-model), habilite o Pool de aplicativos para 32 bits.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-373">For a 32-bit (x86) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) published with a 32-bit SDK that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), enable the Application Pool for 32-bit.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-374">No Gerenciador do IIS, navegue até **pools de aplicativos** na barra lateral **conexões** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-374">In IIS Manager, navigate to **Application Pools** in the **Connections** sidebar.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-375">Selecione o pool de aplicativos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-375">Select the app's Application Pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-376">Na barra lateral **ações** , selecione **Configurações avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-376">In the **Actions** sidebar, select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-377">Defina **habilitar aplicativos de 32 bits** como `True` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-377">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications** to `True`.</span></span> 

   * <span data-ttu-id="496af-378">para uma [implantação autocontida](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) de 64 bits (x64) que usa o [modelo de hospedagem em processo](#in-process-hosting-model), desabilite o pool de aplicativos para processos de 32 bits (x86).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-378">For a 64-bit (x64) [self-contained deployment](/dotnet/core/deploying/#self-contained-deployments-scd) that uses the [in-process hosting model](#in-process-hosting-model), disable the app pool for 32-bit (x86) processes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-379">No Gerenciador do IIS, navegue até **pools de aplicativos** na barra lateral **conexões** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-379">In IIS Manager, navigate to **Application Pools** in the **Connections** sidebar.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-380">Selecione o pool de aplicativos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-380">Select the app's Application Pool.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-381">Na barra lateral **ações** , selecione **Configurações avançadas**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-381">In the **Actions** sidebar, select **Advanced Settings**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-382">Defina **habilitar aplicativos de 32 bits** como `False` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-382">Set **Enable 32-Bit Applications** to `False`.</span></span> 

1. <span data-ttu-id="496af-383">Confirme se a identidade do modelo de processo tem as permissões apropriadas.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-383">Confirm the process model identity has the proper permissions.</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="496af-384">Se a identidade padrão do pool de aplicativos (**modelo de processo**  >  **Identity** ) for alterada **de Identity ApplicationPool** para outra identidade, verifique se a nova identidade tem as permissões necessárias para acessar a pasta, o banco de dados e outros recursos necessários do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-384">If the default identity of the app pool (**Process Model** > **Identity**) is changed from **ApplicationPoolIdentity** to another identity, verify that the new identity has the required permissions to access the app's folder, database, and other required resources.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-385">Por exemplo, o pool de aplicativos requer acesso de leitura e gravação às pastas nas quais o aplicativo lê e grava os arquivos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-385">For example, the app pool requires read and write access to folders where the app reads and writes files.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-386">**Configuração de Autenticação do Windows (opcional)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-386">**Windows Authentication configuration (Optional)**</span></span>  
<span data-ttu-id="496af-387">Para saber mais, veja [Configurar a Autenticação do Windows](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-387">For more information, see [Configure Windows authentication](xref:security/authentication/windowsauth).</span></span>

## <a name="deploy-the-app"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-388">Implantar o aplicativo</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-388">Deploy the app</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-389">Implante o aplicativo na pasta **caminho físico** do IIS que foi estabelecida na seção [Criar o site do IIS](#create-the-iis-site).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-389">Deploy the app to the IIS **Physical path** folder that was established in the [Create the IIS site](#create-the-iis-site) section.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-390">[Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) é o mecanismo recomendado para implantação, mas há várias opções para mover o aplicativo da pasta do projeto `publish` para a pasta de implantação do sistema de hospedagem.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-390">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) is the recommended mechanism for deployment, but several options exist for moving the app from the project's `publish` folder to the hosting system's deployment folder.</span></span>

### <a name="web-deploy-with-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-391">Implantação da Web com o Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-391">Web Deploy with Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-392">Consulte o tópico [Perfis de publicação do Visual Studio para implantação de aplicativos ASP.NET Core](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) para saber como criar um perfil de publicação para uso com a Implantação da Web.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-392">See the [Visual Studio publish profiles for ASP.NET Core app deployment](xref:host-and-deploy/visual-studio-publish-profiles#publish-profiles) topic to learn how to create a publish profile for use with Web Deploy.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-393">Se o provedor de hospedagem fornecer um Perfil de Publicação ou o suporte para a criação de um, baixe o perfil e importe-o usando a caixa de diálogo **Publicar** do Visual Studio:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-393">If the hosting provider provides a Publish Profile or support for creating one, download their profile and import it using the Visual Studio **Publish** dialog:</span></span>

![Página de caixa de diálogo Publicar](index/_static/pub-dialog.png)

### <a name="web-deploy-outside-of-visual-studio"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-395">Implantação da Web fora do Visual Studio</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-395">Web Deploy outside of Visual Studio</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-396">Também é possível usar a [Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) fora do Visual Studio na linha de comando.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-396">[Web Deploy](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/introduction-to-web-deploy) can also be used outside of Visual Studio from the command line.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-397">Para obter mais informações, consulte [Ferramenta de Implantação da Web](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-397">For more information, see [Web Deployment Tool](/iis/publish/using-web-deploy/use-the-web-deployment-tool).</span></span>

### <a name="alternatives-to-web-deploy"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-398">Alternativas à Implantação da Web</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-398">Alternatives to Web Deploy</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-399">Use qualquer um dos vários métodos para mover o aplicativo para o sistema host, como cópia manual, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy) ou [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-399">Use any of several methods to move the app to the hosting system, such as manual copy, [Xcopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/xcopy), [Robocopy](/windows-server/administration/windows-commands/robocopy), or [PowerShell](/powershell/).</span></span>

## <a name="browse-the-website"></a><span data-ttu-id="496af-401">Procurar no site</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-401">Browse the website</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-402">Depois de implantar o aplicativo no sistema de hospedagem, faça uma solicitação para um dos pontos de extremidade públicos do aplicativo.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-402">After the app is deployed to the hosting system, make a request to one of the app's public endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="496af-403">No exemplo a seguir, o site está associado a um **Nome do Host** IIS de `www.mysite.com` na **Porta** `80`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-403">In the following example, the site is bound to an IIS **Host name** of `www.mysite.com` on **Port** `80`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="496af-404">É feita uma solicitação para `http://www.mysite.com`:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="496af-404">A request is made to `http://www.mysite.com`:</span></span>
